md:max-w-[calc(100%_-var(--sidebar-width))]" data-pagefind-body=""><div class="hidden sm:block relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 "><nav aria-label="Breadcrumb" class="py-4 max-w-4xl md:px-4 mb-2"><ol class="flex items-center text-sm"><li><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-started/quickstarts">Home</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/work-with-data">Work with data</a></li><li class="flex class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/work-with-data/publish-data/endpoints">Endpoints</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><span class="font-semibold">Use advanced dynamic endpoint functions</span></li></ol></nav></div><div class="relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]"><div class="max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative" role="main"><article><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between gap-4 mb-6"><h1 id="advanced-template-functions-for-dynamic-api-endpoint" class="t-h3" data-pagefind-weight="20.0">Advanced template functions for dynamic API endpoint<a class="headerlink" href="#advanced-template-functions-for-dynamic-api-endpoint" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h1><div class="flex-shrink-0 w-auto"><div class="relative inline-block w-auto" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex rounded-md overflow-hidden border border-v-border-02 hover:border-v-border-03 transition-colors"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors min-w-[106px] text-v-text-01"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="w-4 h-4 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]"><path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V8z"></path><path d="M14 2v6h6M16 13H8M16 17H8M10 9H8"></path></svg><span>Copy as MD</span></button><button class="flex items-center justify-center px-2 py-1.5 text-sm text-v-text-01 border-l border-v-border-02 min-w-[32px]" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" class="w-3 h-3 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]" style="margin-top:-4px;margin-left:-4px"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><p>Learn how to use <a href="../../../dev-reference/template-functions">template functions</a> to create dynamic API endpoint with Tinybird.</p><h2 id="prerequisites" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Prerequisites<a class="headerlink" href="#prerequisites" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Make sure you&#x27;re familiar with template functions and <a href="../../../work-with-data/query-parameters">query parameters</a>.</p><h2 id="example-data" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Example data<a class="headerlink" href="#example-data" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>This guide uses the eCommerce events data enriched with products. The data looks like the following:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Events and products data">Events and products data</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT *, price, city, day FROM events_mat
ANY LEFT JOIN products_join_sku ON product_id = sku
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="tips-and-tricks" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Tips and tricks<a class="headerlink" href="#tips-and-tricks" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>When the complexity of pipes and API endpoints grows, developing them and knowing what&#x27;s going-on to debug problems can become challenging. Here are some useful tricks for using Tinybird&#x27;s product:</p><h3 id="where-11" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">WHERE 1=1<a class="headerlink" href="#where-11" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>When you filter by different criteria, given by dynamic parameters that can be omitted, you&#x27;ll need a <code>WHERE</code> clause. But if none of the parameters are present, you&#x27;ll need to add a <code>WHERE</code> statement with a dummy condition (like <code>1=1</code>) that&#x27;s always true, and then add the other filter statements dynamically if the parameters are defined, like you do in the <a href="#defined">defined</a> example of this guide.</p><h3 id="use-the-set-function" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Use the set function<a class="headerlink" href="#use-the-set-function" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The <code>set</code> function present in the previous snippet lets you set the value of a parameter in a node, so that you can check the output of a query depending on the value of the parameters it takes. Otherwise, you&#x27;d have to publish an API endpoint and make requests to it with different parameters.</p><p>Using <code>set</code>, you don&#x27;t have to exit the Tinybird UI while creating an API endpoint and the whole process is faster, without needing to go back and forth between your browser or IDE and Postman or cURL.</p><p>Another example of its usage:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Using set to try out different parameter values">Using set to try out different parameter values</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
{% set select_cols = &#x27;date,user_id,event,city&#x27; %}
SELECT
  {{columns(select_cols)}}
FROM events_mat
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>You can use more than one <code>set</code> statement. Put each one on a separate line at the beginning of a node.</p><p><code>set</code> is also a way to set defaults for parameters. If you used <code>set</code> statements to test your API endpoint while developing, remember to remove them before publishing your code, because if not, the <code>set</code> function overrides any incoming parameter.</p><h3 id="default-argument" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Default argument<a class="headerlink" href="#default-argument" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Another way to set default values for parameters is using the <code>default</code> argument that most Tinybird template functions accept. The previous code could be rewritten as follows:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Using the default argument">Using the default argument</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT
  {{columns(select_cols, &#x27;date,user_id,event,city&#x27;)}}
FROM events_mat
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Keep in mind that defining the same parameter in more than one place in your code in different ways can lead to inconsistent behavior. Here&#x27;s a solution to avoid that:</p><h3 id="using-with-statements-to-avoid-duplicating-code" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Using WITH statements to avoid duplicating code<a class="headerlink" href="#using-with-statements-to-avoid-duplicating-code" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>If you plan to use the same dynamic parameters more than once in a node of a pipe, define them in one place to avoid duplicating code. This also makes it clearer which parameters will appear in the node. You can do this with one or more statements at the beginning of a node, using the <code>WITH</code> clause.</p><p>The WITH clause supports CTEs. These are preprocessed before executing the query, and can only return one row. This is different to other databases such as Postgres. For example:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="DRY with the with clause">DRY with the with clause</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
{% set terms=&#x27;orchid&#x27; %}
WITH {{split_to_array(terms, &#x27;1,2,3&#x27;)}} AS needles
SELECT
  *,
  joinGet(products_join_sku, &#x27;color&#x27;, product_id) color,
  joinGet(products_join_sku, &#x27;title&#x27;, product_id) title
FROM events
WHERE
  multiMatchAny(lower(color), needles)
  OR multiMatchAny(lower(title), needles)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="documenting-your-api-endpoints" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Documenting your API endpoints<a class="headerlink" href="#documenting-your-api-endpoints" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Tinybird creates auto-generated documentation for all your published API endpoints, taking the information from the dynamic parameters found in the pipe. It&#x27;s best practice to set default values and descriptions for every parameter in one place (also because some functions don&#x27;t accept a description, for example). This is typically done in the final node, with <code>WITH</code> statements at the beginning. See how to do it in the <a href="#putting-it-all-together">last section</a> of this guide.</p><h3 id="hidden-parameters" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Hidden parameters<a class="headerlink" href="#hidden-parameters" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>If you use some functions like <code>enumerate_with_last</code> in the <a href="#enumerate-with-last">enumarate with last example</a>, you might end up with some variables (called <code>x</code>, <code>last</code> in that code snippet) that Tinybird interprets as if they were parameters that you can set. They appear in the auto-generated documentation page. To avoid that, add a leading underscore to their name, renaming <code>x</code> to <code>_x</code> and <code>last</code> to <code>_last</code>.</p><h2 id="advanced-functions" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Advanced functions<a class="headerlink" href="#advanced-functions" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>The following are practical examples of advanced template functions usage so that it&#x27;s easier for you to understand how to use them.</p><h3 id="defined" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">defined<a class="headerlink" href="#defined" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The <code>defined</code> function lets you check if a query string parameter exists in the request URL or not.</p><p>Imagine you want to filter events with a price within a minimum or a maximum price, set by two dynamic parameters that could be omitted. A way to define the API endpoint would be like this:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="filter by price">filter by price</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
{% set min_price=20 %}
{% set max_price=50 %}

SELECT *, price
FROM events_mat
WHERE 1 = 1
{% if defined(min_price) %}
  AND price &gt;= {{Float32(min_price)}}
{% end %}
{% if defined(max_price) %}
  AND price &lt;= {{Float32(max_price)}}
{% end %}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>To see the effect of having a parameter not defined, use <code>set</code> to set its value to <code>None</code> like this:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="filter by price, price not defined">filter by price, price not defined</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
{% set min_price=None %}
{% set max_price=None %}

SELECT *, price
FROM events_mat
WHERE 1 = 1
{% if defined(min_price) %}
  AND price &gt;= {{Float32(min_price)}}
{% end %}
{% if defined(max_price) %}
  AND price &lt;= {{Float32(max_price)}}
{% end %}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>It&#x27;s also possible to provide smart defaults to avoid needing to use the <code>defined</code> function at all:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="filter by price with default values">filter by price with default values</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT *, price
FROM events_mat_cols
WHERE price &gt;= {{Float32(min_price, 0)}}
  AND price &lt;= {{Float32(max_price, 999999999)}}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arrayvariable-name-type-default" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Array(variable_name, &#x27;type&#x27;, [default])<a class="headerlink" href="#arrayvariable-name-type-default" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Transforms a comma-separated list of values into a Tuple. You can provide a default value for it or not:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT
    {{Array(code, &#x27;UInt32&#x27;, default=&#x27;13412,1234123,4123&#x27;)}} AS codes_1,
    {{Array(code, &#x27;UInt32&#x27;, &#x27;13412,1234123,4123&#x27;)}} AS codes_2,
    {{Array(code, &#x27;UInt32&#x27;)}} AS codes_3
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>To filter events whose type belongs to the ones provided in a dynamic parameter, separated by commas, you&#x27;d define the API endpoint like this:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Filter by list of elements">Filter by list of elements</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT *
FROM events
WHERE event IN {{Array(event_types, &#x27;String&#x27;, default=&#x27;buy,view&#x27;)}}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>And then the URL of the API endpoint would be something like <code>{% user(&quot;apiHost&quot;) %}/v0/pipes/your_pipe_name.json?event_types=buy,view</code></p><h3 id="sql-and" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">sql_and<a class="headerlink" href="#sql-and" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><code>sql_and</code> lets you create a filter with <code>AND</code> operators and several expressions dynamically, taking into account if the dynamic parameters in a template it are present in the request URL.</p><p>It&#x27;s not possible to use Tinybird functions inside the <code>{{ }}</code> brackets in templates. <code>sql_and</code> can only be used with the<code>{column_name}__{operand}</code> syntax. This function does the same as what you saw in the previous query: filtering a column by the values that are present in a tuple generated by <code>Array(...)</code> if <code>operand</code> is <code>in</code>, are greater than (with the <code>gt</code> operand), or less than (with the <code>lt</code> operand). Let&#x27;s see an example to make it clearer:</p><div class="w-full"><div class="bg-bg-darkest rounded-t-md overflow-hidden"><ul role="tablist" class="relative flex justify-start list-none ps-0 before:h-2 before:bg-bg-darkest before:w-full before:absolute before:-bottom-1 before:-z-[1]"><li class="m-0 w-auto"><button role="tab" aria-selected="true" class="py-3 px-4 text-caption text-white transition-all bg-bg-dark font-bold">Endpoint template code</button></li><li class="m-0 w-auto"><button role="tab" aria-selected="false" class="py-3 px-4 text-caption text-white transition-all opacity-60 hover:opacity-100 hover:underline hover:font-bold">Generated SQL</button></li></ul></div><div class="code-tab-content [&amp;_.snippet]:rounded-t-none"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="SQL_AND AND COLUMN__IN">SQL_AND AND COLUMN__IN</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT
  *,
  joinGet(products_join_sku, &#x27;section_id&#x27;, product_id) section_id
FROM events
WHERE {{sql_and(event__in=Array(event_types, &#x27;String&#x27;, default=&#x27;buy,view&#x27;),
                section_id__in=Array(sections, &#x27;Int16&#x27;, default=&#x27;1,2&#x27;))}}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><p>You don&#x27;t have to provide default values. If you set the <code>defined</code> argument of <code>Array</code> to <code>False</code>, when that parameter isn&#x27;t provided, no SQL expression will be generated. You can see this in the next code snippet:</p><div class="w-full"><div class="bg-bg-darkest rounded-t-md overflow-hidden"><ul role="tablist" class="relative flex justify-start list-none ps-0 before:h-2 before:bg-bg-darkest before:w-full before:absolute before:-bottom-1 before:-z-[1]"><li class="m-0 w-auto"><button role="tab" aria-selected="true" class="py-3 px-4 text-caption text-white transition-all bg-bg-dark font-bold">Endpoint template code</button></li><li class="m-0 w-auto"><button role="tab" aria-selected="false" class="py-3 px-4 text-caption text-white transition-all opacity-60 hover:opacity-100 hover:underline hover:font-bold">Generated SQL</button></li></ul></div><div class="code-tab-content [&amp;_.snippet]:rounded-t-none"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="defined=False">defined=False</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT
  *,
  joinGet(products_join_sku, &#x27;section_id&#x27;, product_id) section_id
FROM events
WHERE {{sql_and(event__in=Array(event_types, &#x27;String&#x27;, default=&#x27;buy,view&#x27;),
                section_id__in=Array(sections, &#x27;Int16&#x27;, defined=False))}}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><h3 id="split-to-arrayname-default" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">split_to_array(name, [default])<a class="headerlink" href="#split-to-arrayname-default" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>This works similarly to <code>Array</code>, but it returns an Array of Strings (instead of a tuple). You&#x27;ll have to cast the result to the type you want after. As you can see here too, they behave in a similar way:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="array and split_to_array">array and split_to_array</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT
    {{Array(code, &#x27;UInt32&#x27;, default=&#x27;1,2,3&#x27;)}},
    {{split_to_array(code, &#x27;1,2,3&#x27;)}},
    arrayMap(x-&gt;toInt32(x), {{split_to_array(code, &#x27;1,2,3&#x27;)}}),
    1 in {{Array(code, &#x27;UInt32&#x27;, default=&#x27;1,2,3&#x27;)}},
    &#x27;1&#x27; in {{split_to_array(code, &#x27;1,2,3&#x27;)}}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>One thing that you want to keep in mind is that you can&#x27;t pass non-constant values (arrays, for example) to operations that require them. For example, this would fail:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="using a non-constant expression where one is required">using a non-constant expression where one is required</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT
    1 IN arrayMap(x-&gt;toInt32(x), {{split_to_array(code, &#x27;1,2,3&#x27;)}})
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>If you find an error like this, you should use a Tuple instead (remember that <code>{{Array(...)}}</code> returns a tuple). This will work:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Use a tuple instead">Use a tuple instead</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT
    1 IN {{Array(code, &#x27;Int32&#x27;, default=&#x27;1,2,3&#x27;)}}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p><code>split_to_array</code> is often used with <a href="#enumerate-with-last">enumerate_with_last</a>.</p><h3 id="column-and-columns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">column and columns<a class="headerlink" href="#column-and-columns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>They let you select one or several columns from a data source or pipe, given their name. You can also provide a default value.</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="columns">columns</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT {{columns(cols, &#x27;date,user_id,event&#x27;)}}
FROM events
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="column">column</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT date, {{column(user, &#x27;user_id&#x27;)}}
FROM events
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="enumerate-with-last" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">enumerate_with_last<a class="headerlink" href="#enumerate-with-last" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Creates an iterable array, returning a Boolean value that allows checking if the current element is the last element in the array. Its most common usage is to select several columns, or compute some function over them. See an example of <code>columns</code> and <code>enumerate_with_last</code> here:</p><div class="w-full"><div class="bg-bg-darkest rounded-t-md overflow-hidden"><ul role="tablist" class="relative flex justify-start list-none ps-0 before:h-2 before:bg-bg-darkest before:w-full before:absolute before:-bottom-1 before:-z-[1]"><li class="m-0 w-auto"><button role="tab" aria-selected="true" class="py-3 px-4 text-caption text-white transition-all bg-bg-dark font-bold">Endpoint template code</button></li><li class="m-0 w-auto"><button role="tab" aria-selected="false" class="py-3 px-4 text-caption text-white transition-all opacity-60 hover:opacity-100 hover:underline hover:font-bold">Generated SQL</button></li></ul></div><div class="code-tab-content [&amp;_.snippet]:rounded-t-none"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="enumerate_with_last + columns">enumerate_with_last + columns</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
SELECT
    {% if defined(group_by) %}
        {{columns(group_by)}},
    {% end %}
    sum(price) AS revenue,
    {% for last, x in enumerate_with_last(split_to_array(count_unique_vals_columns, &#x27;section_id,city&#x27;)) %}
        uniq({{symbol(x)}}) as {{symbol(x)}}
        {% if not last %},{% end %}
    {% end %}
  FROM events_enriched
{% if defined(group_by) %}
    GROUP BY
         {{columns(group_by)}}

    ORDER BY
        {{columns(group_by)}}
{% end %}

</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><p>If you use the <code>defined</code> function around a parameter it doesn&#x27;t make sense to give it a default value because if it&#x27;s not provided, that line will never be run.</p><h3 id="error-and-custom-error" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">error and custom_error<a class="headerlink" href="#error-and-custom-error" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>They let you return customized error responses. With <code>error</code> you can customize the error message:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="error">error</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
{% if not defined(event_types) %}
  {{error(&#x27;You need to provide a value for event_types&#x27;)}}
{% end %}
SELECT
  *,
  joinGet(products_join_sku, &#x27;section_id&#x27;, product_id) section_id
FROM events
WHERE event IN {{Array(event_types, &#x27;String&#x27;)}}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="error response using error">error response using error</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">{&quot;error&quot;: &quot;You need to provide a value for event_types&quot;}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>And with <code>custom_error</code> you can also customize the response code:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="custom_error">custom_error</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">%
{% if not defined(event_types) %}
  {{custom_error({&#x27;error&#x27;: &#x27;You need to provide a value for event_types&#x27;, &#x27;code&#x27;: 400})}}
{% end %}
SELECT
  *,
  joinGet(products_join_sku, &#x27;section_id&#x27;, product_id) section_id
FROM events
WHERE event IN {{Array(event_types, &#x27;String&#x27;)}}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="error response using custom_error">error response using custom_error</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">{&quot;error&quot;: &quot;You need to provide a value for event_types&quot;, &quot;code&quot;: 400}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p><strong>Note:</strong> <code>error</code> and <code>custom_error</code> have to be placed at the start of a node or they won&#x27;t work. The order should be:</p><ol><li><code>set</code> lines, to give some parameter a default value (optional)</li><li>Parameter validation functions: <code>error</code> and <code>custom_error</code> <!-- -->definitions</li><li>The SQL query itself</li></ol><h2 id="putting-it-all-together" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Putting it all together<a class="headerlink" href="#putting-it-all-together" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>You&#x27;ve created a pipe where you use most of these advanced techniques to filter ecommerce events.</p><p>This is its code:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="advanced_dynamic_endpoints.pipe">advanced_dynamic_endpoints.pipe</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">NODE events_enriched
SQL &gt;

    SELECT
        *,
        price,
        city,
        day
    FROM events_mat_cols
    ANY LEFT JOIN products_join_sku ON product_id = sku



NODE filter_by_price
SQL &gt;

    %
        SELECT * FROM events_enriched
        WHERE 1 = 1
        {% if defined(min_price) %}
          AND price &gt;= {{Float32(min_price)}}
        {% end %}
        {% if defined(max_price) %}
          AND price &lt;= {{Float32(max_price)}}
        {% end %}



NODE filter_by_event_type_and_section_id
SQL &gt;

    %
    SELECT
          *
        FROM filter_by_price
        {% if defined(event_types) or defined(section_ids) %} ...
            WHERE {{sql_and(event__in=Array(event_types, &#x27;String&#x27;, defined=False, enum=[&#x27;remove_item_from_cart&#x27;,&#x27;view&#x27;,&#x27;search&#x27;,&#x27;buy&#x27;,&#x27;add_item_to_cart&#x27;]),
                            section_id__in=Array(section_ids, &#x27;Int32&#x27;, defined=False))}}
        {% end %}



NODE filter_by_title_or_color
SQL &gt;

    %
    SELECT *
    FROM filter_by_event_type_and_section_id
    {% if defined(search_terms) %}
    WHERE
      multiMatchAny(lower(color), {{split_to_array(search_terms)}})
      OR multiMatchAny(lower(title), {{split_to_array(search_terms)}})
    {% end %}



NODE group_by_or_not
SQL &gt;

    %
        SELECT
            {% if defined(group_by) %}
              {{columns(group_by)}},
              sum(price) AS revenue,
              {% for _last, _x in enumerate_with_last(split_to_array(count_unique_vals_columns)) %}
                  uniq({{symbol(_x)}}) as {{symbol(_x)}}
                  {% if not _last %},{% end %}
              {% end %}
            {% else %}
              *
            {% end %}
        FROM filter_by_title_or_color
        {% if defined(group_by) %}
            GROUP BY {{columns(group_by)}}
            ORDER BY {{columns(group_by)}}
        {% end %}



NODE pagination
SQL &gt;

    %
    WITH
      {{Array(group_by,
      &#x27;String&#x27;,
      &#x27;&#x27;,
               description=&#x27;Comma-separated name of columns. If defined, group by and order the results by these columns. The sum of revenue will be returned&#x27;)}},
      {{Array(count_unique_vals_columns, &#x27;String&#x27;, &#x27;&#x27;,
               description=&#x27;Comma-separated name of columns. If both group_by and count_unique_vals_columns are defined, the number of unique values in the columns given in count_unique_vals_columns will be returned as well&#x27;)}},
       {{Array(search_terms, &#x27;String&#x27;, &#x27;&#x27;,
              description=&#x27;Comma-separated list of search terms present in the color or title of products&#x27;)}},
       {{Array(event_types, &#x27;String&#x27;, &#x27;&#x27;,
               description=&quot;Comma-separated list of event name types&quot;, enum=[&#x27;remove_item_from_cart&#x27;,&#x27;view&#x27;,&#x27;search&#x27;,&#x27;buy&#x27;,&#x27;add_item_to_cart&#x27;])}},
       {{Array(section_ids, &#x27;String&#x27;, &#x27;&#x27;,
               description=&quot;Comma-separated list of section IDs. The minimum value for an ID is 0 and the max is 50.&quot;)}}
    SELECT * FROM group_by_or_not
    LIMIT {{Int32(page_size, 100)}}
    OFFSET {{Int32(page, 0) * Int32(page_size, 100)}}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>To replicate it in your account, copy the previous code to a new endpoint file called <code>advanced_dynamic_endpoints.pipe</code> locally and deploy your changes.</p></article><div class="flex items-center justify-end h-10" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="italic text-caption"><span>Updated<!-- --> <time "default\"]\n43:I[57187,[\"5878\",\"static/chunks/9da6db1e-fe3f3691e817470b.js\",\"314\",\"static/chunks/32ea55aa-334b9848c750da09.js\",\"4960\",\"static/chunks/8b30ef62-8e1a3557163ef34d.js\",\"9729\",\"static/chunks/72b2f85d-e46ed6c2f9c8d9d7.js\",\"5501\",\"static/chunks/c16f53c3-0400c7825a916970.js\",\"8370\",\"static/chunks/8370-7a9554878d1b9d35.js\",\"7648\",\"static/chunks/7648-2c0c3a3dc3702719.js\",\"2694\",\"static/chunks/2694-6ee008eb8be89699.js\",\"9267\",\"static/chunks/9267-89ff5dc708370f39.js\",\"1284\",\"static/chunks/1284-f30446673b9ba073.js\",\"7867\",\"static/chunks/7867-6d0484accd87a171.js\",\"3145\",\"static/chunks/3145-ca0c40eb1bb881d8.js\",\"5107\",\"static/chunks/5107-ef688f2fbbe55825.js\",\"2418\",\"static/chunks/2418-b0d27e6f47546ed6.js\",\"4144\",\"static/chunks/4144-34f98e6e70550e12.js\",\"1147\",\"static/chunks/1147-ac53c80b8f8a3921.js\",\"1749\",\"static/chunks/1749-b2df567f1b8974df.js\",\"5643\",\"static/chunks/5643-5ba78075e5c8bae2.js\",\"1796\",\"static/chunks/1796-b956fe6fe21dbf17.js\",\"787\",\"static/chunks/787-09fc1907ef45c351.js\",\"996\",\"static/chunks/996-ce0ceee74ea8f43a.js\",\"7432\",\"static/chunks/7432-03643de0998568d4.js\",\"1384\",\"static/chunks/app/(forward)/forward/%5B%5B...slug%5D%5D/page-8347ce85311902e7.js\"],\"default\"]\n21:T4196,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"---\ntitle: Advanced template functions for dynamic API endpoint\nmeta:\n  description: Learn more about creating dynamic API endpoint using advanced templates.\nheadingMaxLevels: 2\n---\n\n# Advanced template functions for dynamic API endpoint\n\nLearn how to use [template functions](../../../dev-reference/template-functions) to create dynamic API endpoint with Tinybird.\n\n## Prerequisites\n\nMake sure you're familiar with template functions and [query parameters](../../../work-with-data/query-parameters).\n\n## Example data\n\nThis guide uses the eCommerce events data enriched with products. The data looks like the following:\n\n```sql {% title=\"Events and products data\"  %}\nSELECT *, price, city, day FROM events_mat\nANY LEFT JOIN products_join_sku ON product_id = sku\n```\n\n## Tips and tricks\n\nWhen the complexity of pipes and API endpoints grows, developing them and knowing what's going-on to debug problems can become challenging. Here are some useful tricks for using Tinybird's product:\n\n### WHERE 1=1\n\nWhen you filter by different criteria, given by dynamic parameters that can be omitted, you'll need a `WHERE` clause. But if none of the parameters are present, you'll need to add a `WHERE` statement with a dummy condition (like `1=1`) that's always true, and then add the other filter statements dynamically if the parameters are defined, like you do in the [defined](#defined) example of this guide.\n\n### Use the set function\n\nThe `set` function present in the previous snippet lets you set the value of a parameter in a node, so that you can check the output of a query depending on the value of the parameters it takes. Otherwise, you'd have to publish an API endpoint and make requests to it with different parameters.\n\nUsing `set`, you don't have to exit the Tinybird UI while creating an API endpoint and the whole process is faster, without needing to go back and forth between your browser or IDE and Postman or cURL.\n\nAnother example of its usage:\n\n```sql {% title=\"Using set to try out different parameter values\"  %}\n%\n{\\% set select_cols = 'date,user_id,event,city' %}\nSELECT\n  {{columns(select_cols)}}\nFROM events_mat\n```\n\nYou can use more than one `set` statement. Put each one on a separate line at the beginning of a node.\n\n`set` is also a way to set defaults for parameters. If you used `set` statements to test your API endpoint while developing, remember to remove them before publishing your code, because if not, the `set` function overrides any incoming parameter.\n\n### Default argument\n\nAnother way to set default values for parameters is using the `default` argument that most Tinybird template functions accept. The previous code could be rewritten as follows:\n\n```sql {% title=\"Using the default argument\"  %}\n%\nSELECT\n  {{columns(select_cols, 'date,user_id,event,city')}}\nFROM events_mat\n```\n\nKeep in mind that defining the same parameter in more than one place in your code in different ways can lead to inconsistent behavior. Here's a solution to avoid that:\n\n### Using WITH statements to avoid duplicating code\n\nIf you plan to use the same dynamic parameters more than once in a node of a pipe, define them in one place to avoid duplicating code. This also makes it clearer which parameters will appear in the node. You can do this with one or more statements at the beginning of a node, using the `WITH` clause.\n\nThe WITH clause supports CTEs. These are preprocessed before executing the query, and can only return one row. This is different to other databases such as Postgres. For example:\n\n```sql {% title=\"DRY with the with clause\"  %}\n%\n{\\% set terms='orchid' %}\nWITH {{split_to_array(terms, '1,2,3')}} AS needles\nSELECT\n  *,\n  joinGet(products_join_sku, 'color', product_id) color,\n  joinGet(products_join_sku, 'title', product_id) title\nFROM events\nWHERE\n  multiMatchAny(lower(color), needles)\n  OR multiMatchAny(lower(title), needles)\n```\n\n### Documenting your API endpoints\n\nTinybird creates auto-generated documentation for all your published API endpoints, taking the information from the dynamic parameters found in the pipe. It's best practice to set default values and descriptions for every parameter in one place (also because some functions don't accept a description, for example). This is typically done in the final node, with `WITH` statements at the beginning. See how to do it in the [last section](#putting-it-all-together) of this guide.\n\n### Hidden parameters\n\nIf you use some functions like `enumerate_with_last` in the [enumarate with last example](#enumerate-with-last), you might end up with some variables (called `x`, `last` in that code snippet) that Tinybird interprets as if they were parameters that you can set. They appear in the auto-generated documentation page. To avoid that, add a leading underscore to their name, renaming `x` to `_x` and `last` to `_last`.\n\n## Advanced functions\n\nThe following are practical examples of advanced template functions usage so that it's easier for you to understand how to use them.\n\n### defined\n\nThe `defined` function lets you check if a query string parameter exists in the request URL or not.\n\nImagine you want to filter events with a price within a minimum or a maximum price, set by two dynamic parameters that could be omitted. A way to define the API endpoint would be like this:\n\n```sql {% title=\"filter by price\"  %}\n%\n{\\% set min_price=20 %}\n{\\% set max_price=50 %}\n\nSELECT *, price\nFROM events_mat\nWHERE 1 = 1\n{\\% if defined(min_price) %}\n  AND price \u003e= {{Float32(min_price)}}\n{\\% end %}\n{\\% if defined(max_price) %}\n  AND price \u003c= {{Float32(max_price)}}\n{\\% end %}\n```\n\nTo see the effect of having a parameter not defined, use `set` to set its value to `None` like this:\n\n```sql {% title=\"filter by price, price not defined\"  %}\n%\n{\\% set min_price=None %}\n{\\% set max_price=None %}\n\nSELECT *, price\nFROM events_mat\nWHERE 1 = 1\n{\\% if defined(min_price) %}\n  AND price \u003e= {{Float32(min_price)}}\n{\\% end %}\n{\\% if defined(max_price) %}\n  AND price \u003c= {{Float32(max_price)}}\n{\\% end %}\n```\n\nIt's also possible to provide smart defaults to avoid needing to use the `defined` function at all:\n\n```sql {% title=\"filter by price with default values\" %}\n%\nSELECT *, price\nFROM events_mat_cols\nWHERE price \u003e= {{Float32(min_price, 0)}}\n  AND price \u003c= {{Float32(max_price, 999999999)}}\n```\n\n### Array(variable_name, 'type', [default])\n\nTransforms a comma-separated list of values into a Tuple. You can provide a default value for it or not:\n\n```sql\n%\nSELECT\n    {{Array(code, 'UInt32', default='13412,1234123,4123')}} AS codes_1,\n    {{Array(code, 'UInt32', '13412,1234123,4123')}} AS codes_2,\n    {{Array(code, 'UInt32')}} AS codes_3\n```\n\nTo filter events whose type belongs to the ones provided in a dynamic parameter, separated by commas, you'd define the API endpoint like this:\n\n```sql {% title=\"Filter by list of elements\"  %}\n%\nSELECT *\nFROM events\nWHERE event IN {{Array(event_types, 'String', default='buy,view')}}\n```\n\nAnd then the URL of the API endpoint would be something like `{% user(\"apiHost\") %}/v0/pipes/your_pipe_name.json?event_types=buy,view`\n\n### sql_and\n\n`sql_and` lets you create a filter with `AND` operators and several expressions dynamically, taking into account if the dynamic parameters in a template it are present in the request URL.\n\nIt's not possible to use Tinybird functions inside the `{{ }}` brackets in templates. `sql_and` can only be used with the`{column_name}__{operand}` syntax. This function does the same as what you saw in the previous query: filtering a column by the values that are present in a tuple generated by `Array(...)` if `operand` is `in`, are greater than (with the `gt` operand), or less than (with the `lt` operand). Let's see an example to make it clearer:\n\n{% tabs %}\n\n{% tab label=\"Endpoint template code\"  %}\n\n```sql {% title=\"SQL_AND AND COLUMN__IN\"  %}\n%\nSELECT\n  *,\n  joinGet(products_join_sku, 'section_id', product_id) section_id\nFROM events\nWHERE {{sql_and(event__in=Array(event_types, 'String', default='buy,view'),\n                section_id__in=Array(sections, 'Int16', default='1,2'))}}\n```\n\n{% /tab %}\n\n{% tab label=\"Generated SQL\" %}\n\n```sql {% title=\"SQL_AND AND COLUMN__IN\"  %}\nSELECT\n    *,\n    joinGet(products_join_sku, 'section_id', product_id) AS section_id\nFROM events\nWHERE (event IN ('buy', 'view')) AND (section_id IN (1, 2))\n```\n\n{% /tab %}\n\n{% /tabs %}\n\nYou don't have to provide default values. If you set the `defined` argument of `Array` to `False`, when that parameter isn't provided, no SQL expression will be generated. You can see this in the next code snippet:\n\n\n{% tabs %}\n\n{% tab label=\"Endpoint template code\"  %}\n\n```sql {% title=\"defined=False\"  %}\n%\nSELECT\n  *,\n  joinGet(products_join_sku, 'section_id', product_id) section_id\nFROM events\nWHERE {{sql_and(event__in=Array(event_types, 'String', default='buy,view'),\n                section_id__in=Array(sections, 'Int16', defined=False))}}\n```\n\n{% /tab %}\n\n{% tab label=\"Generated SQL\" %}\n\n```sql {% title=\"defined=False\"  %}\nSELECT\n    *,\n    joinGet(products_join_sku, 'section_id', product_id) AS section_id\nFROM events\nWHERE event IN ('buy', 'view')\n```\n\n{% /tab %}\n\n{% /tabs %}\n\n### split_to_array(name, [default])\n\nThis works similarly to `Array`, but it returns an Array of Strings (instead of a tuple). You'll have to cast the result to the type you want after. As you can see here too, they behave in a similar way:\n\n```sql {% title=\"array and split_to_array\"  %}\n%\nSELECT\n    {{Array(code, 'UInt32', default='1,2,3')}},\n    {{split_to_array(code, '1,2,3')}},\n    arrayMap(x-\u003etoInt32(x), {{split_to_array(code, '1,2,3')}}),\n    1 in {{Array(code, 'UInt32', default='1,2,3')}},\n    '1' in {{split_to_array(code, '1,2,3')}}\n```\n\nOne thing that you want to keep in mind is that you can't pass non-constant values (arrays, for example) to operations that require them. For example, this would fail:\n\n```sql {% title=\"using a non-constant expression where one is required\"  %}\n%\nSELECT\n    1 IN arrayMap(x-\u003etoInt32(x), {{split_to_array(code, '1,2,3')}})\n```\n\nIf you find an error like this, you should use a Tuple instead (remember that `{{Array(...)}}` returns a tuple). This will work:\n\n```sql {% title=\"Use a tuple instead\"  %}\n%\nSELECT\n    1 IN {{Array(code, 'Int32', default='1,2,3')}}\n```\n\n`split_to_array` is often used with [enumerate_with_last](#enumerate-with-last).\n\n### column and columns\n\nThey let you select one or several columns from a data source or pipe, given their name. You can also provide a default value.\n\n```sql {% title=\"columns\"  %}\n%\nSELECT {{columns(cols, 'date,user_id,event')}}\nFROM events\n```\n\n```sql {% title=\"column\"  %}\n%\nSELECT date, {{column(user, 'user_id')}}\nFROM events\n```\n\n### enumerate_with_last\n\nCreates an iterable array, returning a Boolean value that allows checking if the current element is the last element in the array. Its most common usage is to select several columns, or compute some function over them. See an example of `columns` and `enumerate_with_last` here:\n\n\n{% tabs %}\n\n{% tab label=\"Endpoint template code\"  %}\n\n```sql {% title=\"enumerate_with_last + columns\" %}\n%\nSELECT\n    {\\% if defined(group_by) %}\n        {{columns(group_by)}},\n    {\\% end %}\n    sum(price) AS revenue,\n    {\\% for last, x in enumerate_with_last(split_to_array(count_unique_vals_columns, 'section_id,city')) %}\n        uniq({{symbol(x)}}) as {{symbol(x)}}\n        {\\% if not last %},{\\% end %}\n    {\\% end %}\n  FROM events_enriched\n{\\% if defined(group_by) %}\n    GROUP BY\n         {{columns(group_by)}}\n\n    ORDER BY\n        {{columns(group_by)}}\n{\\% end %}\n\n```\n\n{% /tab %}\n\n{% tab label=\"Generated SQL\" %}\n\n```sql {% title=\"enumerate_with_last + columns\" %}\n-- given that group_by=day and count_unique_cals_columns=section_id,city\n\nSELECT\n    day,\n    sum(price) AS revenue,\n    uniq(section_id) AS section_id,\n    uniq(city) AS city\nFROM events_enriched\nGROUP BY day\nORDER BY day ASC\n```\n\n{% /tab %}\n\n{% /tabs %}\n\nIf you use the `defined` function around a parameter it doesn't make sense to give it a default value because if it's not provided, that line will never be run.\n\n### error and custom_error\n\nThey let you return customized error responses. With `error` you can customize the error message:\n\n```sql {% title=\"error\" %}\n%\n{\\% if not defined(event_types) %}\n  {{error('You need to provide a value for event_types')}}\n{\\% end %}\nSELECT\n  *,\n  joinGet(products_join_sku, 'section_id', product_id) section_id\nFROM events\nWHERE event IN {{Array(event_types, 'String')}}\n```\n\n```json {% title=\"error response using error\" %}\n{\"error\": \"You need to provide a value for event_types\"}\n```\n\nAnd with `custom_error` you can also customize the response code:\n\n```sql {% title=\"custom_error\" %}\n%\n{\\% if not defined(event_types) %}\n  {{custom_error({'error': 'You need to provide a value for event_types', 'code': 400})}}\n{\\% end %}\nSELECT\n  *,\n  joinGet(products_join_sku, 'section_id', product_id) section_id\nFROM events\nWHERE event IN {{Array(event_types, 'String')}}\n```\n\n```json {% title=\"error response using custom_error\" %}\n{\"error\": \"You need to provide a value for event_types\", \"code\": 400}\n```\n\n**Note:** `error` and `custom_error` have to be placed at the start of a node or they won't work. The order should be:\n\n1.  `set` lines, to give some parameter a default value (optional)\n2.  Parameter validation functions: `error` and `custom_error`\n    definitions\n3.  The SQL query itself\n\n## Putting it all together\n\nYou've created a pipe where you use most of these advanced techniques to filter ecommerce events.\n\nThis is its code:\n\n```sql {% title=\"advanced_dynamic_endpoints.pipe\" %}\nNODE events_enriched\nSQL \u003e\n\n    SELECT\n        *,\n        price,\n        city,\n        day\n    FROM events_mat_cols\n    ANY LEFT JOIN products_join_sku ON product_id = sku\n\n\n\nNODE filter_by_price\nSQL \u003e\n\n    %\n        SELECT * FROM events_enriched\n        WHERE 1 = 1\n        {\\% if defined(min_price) %}\n          AND price \u003e= {{Float32(min_price)}}\n        {\\% end %}\n        {\\% if defined(max_price) %}\n          AND price \u003c= {{Float32(max_price)}}\n        {\\% end %}\n\n\n\nNODE filter_by_event_type_and_section_id\nSQL \u003e\n\n    %\n    SELECT\n          *\n        FROM filter_by_price\n        {\\% if defined(event_types) or defined(section_ids) %} ...\n            WHERE {{sql_and(event__in=Array(event_types, 'String', defined=False, enum=['remove_item_from_cart','view','search','buy','add_item_to_cart']),\n                            section_id__in=Array(section_ids, 'Int32', defined=False))}}\n        {\\% end %}\n\n\n\nNODE filter_by_title_or_color\nSQL \u003e\n\n    %\n    SELECT *\n    FROM filter_by_event_type_and_section_id\n    {\\% if defined(search_terms) %}\n    WHERE\n      multiMatchAny(lower(color), {{split_to_array(search_terms)}})\n      OR multiMatchAny(lower(title), {{split_to_array(search_terms)}})\n    {\\% end %}\n\n\n\nNODE group_by_or_not\nSQL \u003e\n\n    %\n        SELECT\n            {\\% if defined(group_by) %}\n              {{columns(group_by)}},\n              sum(price) AS revenue,\n              {\\% for _last, _x in enumerate_with_last(split_to_array(count_unique_vals_columns)) %}\n                  uniq({{symbol(_x)}}) as {{symbol(_x)}}\n                  {\\% if not _last %},{\\% end %}\n              {\\% end %}\n            {\\% else %}\n              *\n            {\\% end %}\n        FROM filter_by_title_or_color\n        {\\% if defined(group_by) %}\n            GROUP BY {{columns(group_by)}}\n            ORDER BY {{columns(group_by)}}\n        {\\% end %}\n\n\n\nNODE pagination\nSQL \u003e\n\n    %\n    WITH\n      {{Array(group_by,\n      'String',\n      '',\n               description='Comma-separated name of columns. If defined, group by and order the results by these columns. The sum of revenue will be returned')}},\n      {{Array(count_unique_vals_columns, 'String', '',\n               description='Comma-separated name of columns. If both group_by and count_unique_vals_columns are defined, the number of unique values in the columns given in count_unique_vals_columns will be returned as well')}},\n       {{Array(search_terms, 'String', '',\n              description='Comma-separated list of search terms present in the color or title of products')}},\n       {{Array(event_types, 'String', '',\n               description=\"Comma-separated list of event name types\", enum=['remove_item_from_cart','view','search','buy','add_item_to_cart'])}},\n       {{Array(section_ids, 'String', '',\n               description=\"Comma-separated list of section IDs. The minimum value for an ID is 0 and the max is 50.\")}}\n    SELECT * FROM group_by_or_not\n    LIMIT {{Int32(page_size, 100)}}\n    OFFSET {{Int32(page, 0) * Int32(page_size, 100)}}\n```\n\nTo replicate it in your account, copy the previous code to a new endpoint file called `advanced_dynamic_endpoints.pipe` locally and deploy your changes.\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"8:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative\",\"role\":\"main\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L20\",null,{\"pageContent\":\"$21\",\"pagePath\":\"docs/work-with-data/publish-data/guides/advanced-dynamic-endpoints-functions\",\"children\":[\"$\",\"article\",null,{\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":1,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"Advanced template functions for dynamic API endpoint\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":[\"Learn how to use \",[\"$\",\"$L23\",null,{\"href\":\"../../../dev-reference/template-functions\",\"prefetch\":false,\"children\":\"template functions\"}],\" to create dynamic API endpoint with Tinybird.\"]}],[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":2,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"Prerequisites\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":[\"Make sure you're familiar with template functions and \",[\"$\",\"$L23\",null,{\"href\":\"../../../work-with-data/query-parameters\",\"prefetch\":false,\"children\":\"query parameters\"}],\".\"]}],[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":2,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"Example data\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":\"This guide uses the eCommerce events data enriched with products. This will work:\"]}],\"$L35\",[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":[[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"split_to_array\"}],\" is often used with \",[\"$\",\"$L23\",null,{\"href\":\"#enumerate-with-last\",\"prefetch\":false,\"children\":\"enumerate_with_last\"}],\".\"]}],[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":3,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"column and columns\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":\"They let you select one or several columns from a data source or pipe, given their name.
